<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“乐器”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">C+1000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本质：特异本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：物品改造</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">重量：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：这是一个画着企鹅的创可贴。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">幻化乐器：你可以对任意一个分类为武器的物品贴上本改造，这会使得目标武器获得【回声】特性。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">此外，你可以以一个移动动作使得该武器在外观上变成某种乐器（吉他</font><font face="宋体">/贝斯/架子鼓/键盘/麦克风），这仅会改变目标武器的外观，不会改变目标武器的具体数值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">没有美少女的乐队番谁看啊？：你的表达检定获得你倾城之貌专长等级</font><font face="宋体">/点附加成功。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">加油练习：你持用接受本改造的武器时，你的表达检定获得</font><font face="宋体">12DP器械加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-ansi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
